# Text Elements
Conduction ^YOgy6iU3

Convection ^p8UwyDUo

Radiation Reflectors ^sqMuzeZ3

-> Happens Mostly in solids

: Thermal conduction in all solids occurs due to the vibration or movement
of atom/molecules in a lattice.
-> Free delocalised electrons ^lBhI3ZxR

-> Only in Liquids and Gases
    - They have free flowing particles
-> It is the process in which, The heat provided
causes the energetically charged particles to become less dense
and flow upwards. Vice versa the less dense particles
flow down, Hence creating a convection current ^GcIX8NnQ

-> This is the energy transfer due to infra red radiation
    - It can happen in any medium
    Whether it is in a vacuum, air, water
Every body is capable of Absorbing/Reflecting Radiation ^5S8erWWQ

Radiation ^fxUYeaAy

Color -> White Surfaces
Texture -> Shiny surface ^Rlhk6zAE

Radiation Absorbers ^9E6GqQGM

Color -> Dark Surface
Texture -> Dull surface ^RF8K9KHs
